defined_text = { 
	name = Rights_Subject
	text = { 
		localisation_key = Rights_Citizen
		trigger = { 
			government = republic
		}
	}
	text = { 
		localisation_key = Rights_Subject
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { 
				government = republic
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
}

	name = Reqs_HasNOStatesman
	text = {

			AND = {

							ai = yes
